aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/search"><span>How-to: Query &amp; Search</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Vector similarity search</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Vector similarity search</h1></header><p>Vector search returns the objects with most similar vectors to that of the query.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Prefer natural language queries?</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>The <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/query-agent">Query Agent</a> translates plain English questions into optimized Weaviate queries automatically - no manual query construction needed.</p><span class="cloudOnlyBadge_iHZd compact_l2tC"><img src="/img/cloud-icon.svg" alt="" class="cloudIcon_a1CI"><span>Cloud only</span></span></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="search-with-text">Search with text<a href="#search-with-text" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Search with text" title="Direct link to Search with text" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators#neartext"><code>Near Text</code></a> operator to find objects with the nearest vector to an input text.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="graphql">GraphQL</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="search-with-image">Search with image<a href="#search-with-image" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Search with image" title="Direct link to Search with image" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<p>Use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators"><code>Near Image</code></a> operator to find objects with the nearest vector to an image.<br>
This example uses a base64 representation of an image.</p>

<p>See <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/image">Image search</a> for more information.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="search-with-an-existing-object">Search with an existing object<a href="#search-with-an-existing-object" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Search with an existing object" title="Direct link to Search with an existing object" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>If you have an object ID, use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators#nearobject"><code>Near Object</code></a> operator to find similar objects to that object.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="search-with-a-vector">Search with a vector<a href="#search-with-a-vector" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Search with a vector" title="Direct link to Search with a vector" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>If you have an input vector, use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators#nearvector"><code>Near Vector</code></a> operator to find objects with similar vectors</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="named-vectors">Named vectors<a href="#named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Named vectors" title="Direct link to Named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.24</code></div></div>
<p>To search a collection that has <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#named-vectors">named vectors</a>, use the <code>target vector</code> field to specify which named vector to search.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="set-a-similarity-threshold">Set a similarity threshold<a href="#set-a-similarity-threshold" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Set a similarity threshold" title="Direct link to Set a similarity threshold" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To set a similarity threshold between the search and target vectors, define a maximum <code>distance</code> (or <code>certainty</code>).</p>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Additional information</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><ul>
<li class="">The distance value depends on many factors, including the vectorization model you use. Experiment with your data to find a value that works for you.</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/distances#distance-vs-certainty"><code>certainty</code></a> is only available with <code>cosine</code> distance.</li>
<li class="">To find the least similar objects, use the negative cosine distance with <code>nearVector</code> search.</li>
</ul></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="limit--offset"><code>limit</code> &amp; <code>offset</code><a href="#limit--offset" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to limit--offset" title="Direct link to limit--offset" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>limit</code> to set a fixed maximum number of objects to return.</p>
<p>Optionally, use <code>offset</code> to paginate the results.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="limit-result-groups">Limit result groups<a href="#limit-result-groups" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Limit result groups" title="Direct link to Limit result groups" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To limit results to groups of similar distances to the query, use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/additional-operators#autocut"><code>autocut</code></a> filter to set the number of groups to return.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="group-results">Group results<a href="#group-results" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Group results" title="Direct link to Group results" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Use a property or a cross-reference to group results. To group returned objects, the query must include a <code>Near</code> search operator, such as <code>Near Text</code> or <code>Near Object</code>.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-results">Filter results<a href="#filter-results" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter results" title="Direct link to Filter results" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>For more specific results, use a <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/filters"><code>filter</code></a> to narrow your search.</p>
